					NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_french_navy }
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_the_french_air_force }
				}
				add_ideas = FRA_idea_military_improvement_army
			}
			if = { #If Air Force has been taken
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_french_navy }
					has_completed_focus = FRA_the_french_air_force
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = FRA_idea_military_improvement_air_force
					add_idea = FRA_idea_military_improvement_army_and_air_force
				}
			}
			if = { #If Navy has been taken
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = FRA_the_french_air_force }
					has_completed_focus = FRA_french_navy
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = FRA_idea_military_improvement_navy
					add_idea = FRA_idea_military_improvement_army_and_navy
				}
			}
			if = { #If BOTH Air Force and Navy been taken
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = FRA_french_navy
					has_completed_focus = FRA_the_french_air_force
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = FRA_idea_military_improvement_air_force_and_navy
					add_idea = FRA_idea_the_french_military
				} #The Military has reached full reform!
			}
			set_temp_variable = { treasury_change = -10 }
			modify_treasury_effect = yes
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.1
				NOT = { has_global_flag = FRA_CHAOS_PATH }
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				NOT = { has_global_flag = FRA_CHAOS_PATH }
				has_war = no
				has_government = neutrality
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				NOT = { has_global_flag = FRA_CHAOS_PATH }
				has_government = nationalist
			}
		}

				}
			}
